-----------------------------\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Optimize an existing MIDI script by removing redundant CC messages and merging open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or num_harmonics=8):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze a .wav file and generate a synthesizer data text file containing:\n    - Detected fundamental frequency (pitch)\n    - Envelope (attack, decay, sustain, np.argmax(env > 0.05 * np.max(env))\n    decay_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.8 * np.max(env))\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * np.max(env)) - 1\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else np.max(env)\n\n    # Fundamental frequency detection (FFT peak)\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    # Harmonics\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag)))\n\n    # Save to text file\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from Analyzing user-provided .Wav files to extract audio features and generate\n   synthesizer data text files.\n3. Fine-tuning virtual instrument configurations for DAWs.\n4. Producing an explanatory document of the generated configurations.\n\nDependencies:\n- mido\n- soundfile\n- numpy\n- scipy\n- librosa\n\nInstall dependencies with:\npip install mido python-rtmidi soundfile numpy scipy librosa\n\nAuthor: [Your Name]\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport sys\nimport glob\nimport json\nimport mido\nimport soundfile as sf\nimport numpy as np\nimport librosa\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# ----------------------------- MIDI Script Optimizer -----------------------------\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(script_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Reads a Python script, identifies inefficient MIDI input handling patterns,\n    and suggests or applies optimizations.\n    \"\"\"\n    with open(script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    issues_found = []\n    for i, line in enumerate(lines):\n        # Example: Replace time.sleep polling with mido's iter_pending\n        if 'time.sleep' in line and 'mido' in ''.join(lines[:i]):\n            issues_found.append((i, 'Polling MIDI input with time.sleep; consider using mido.ports.Input().iter_pending()'))\n            # Suggest replacing with efficient event loop (not auto-fix for safety)\n        optimized_lines.append(line)\n\n    # Save the optimized script (if any changes)\n    optimized_script_path = script_path.replace('.py', '_optimized.py')\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(optimized_lines)\n\n    return optimized_script_path, issues_found\n\n# ------------------------ .Wav File Analyzer & Synth Data ------------------------\n\ndef analyze_wav_and_generate_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyzes a .wav file and generates a text file containing synthesizer data:\n    - Fundamental frequency\n    - Detected notes\n    - Envelope (ADSR estimation)\n    - Spectral centroid\n    \"\"\"\n    y, sr = librosa.load(wav_path, sr=None, mono=True)\n    duration = librosa.get_duration(y=y, sr=sr)\n\n    # Pitch detection\n    pitches, magnitudes = librosa.piptrack(y=y, sr=sr)\n    pitch_values = []\n    for i in range(pitches.shape[1]):\n        index = magnitudes[:, i].argmax()\n        pitch = pitches[index, i]\n        if pitch > 0:\n            pitch_values.append(pitch)\n    if pitch_values:\n        fundamental_freq = np.median(pitch_values)\n    else:\n        fundamental_freq = 0\n\n    # Note estimation\n    midi_notes = [librosa.hz_to_midi(p) for p in pitch_values if p > 0]\n    midi_notes = [int(round(n)) for n in midi_notes]\n    detected_notes = list(sorted(set(midi_notes)))\n\n    # Envelope estimation (ADSR)\n    envelope = np.abs(librosa.onset.onset_strength(y=y, sr=sr))\n    attack = np.argmax(envelope > 0.1 * np.max(envelope)) / sr\n    decay = np.argmax(envelope > 0.9 * np.max(envelope)) / sr - attack\n    sustain_level = np.mean(envelope[int(0.5*len(envelope)):])\n    release = duration - (attack + decay)\n\n    # Spectral centroid\n    spectral_centroids = librosa.feature.spectral_centroid(y=y, sr=sr)[0]\n    avg_centroid = np.mean(spectral_centroids)\n\n    # Write synth data file\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental Frequency: {fundamental_freq:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Detected MIDI Notes: {detected_notes}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope (ADSR, seconds):\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {decay:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {release:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Spectral Centroid: {avg_centroid:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n\n    return {\n        'fundamental_freq': fundamental_freq,\n        'detected_notes': detected_notes,\n        'envelope': {'attack': attack, 'decay': decay, 'sustain': sustain_level, 'release': release},\n        'spectral_centroid': avg_centroid\n    }\n\n# --------------------- Virtual Instrument Configuration Tuner --------------------\n\ndef fine_tune_virtual_instrument(synth_data, config_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generates a JSON configuration for a virtual instrument based on the analyzed synth data.\n    \"\"\"\n    config = {\n        \"oscillator\": {\n            \"type\": \"sine\" if synth_data['spectral_centroid'] < 1500 else \"saw\",\n            \"frequency\": synth_data['fundamental_freq']\n        },\n        \"envelope\": synth_data['envelope'],\n        \"notes\": synth_data['detected_notes'],\n        \"filter\": {\n            \"cutoff\": synth_data['spectral_centroid'],\n            \"resonance\": 0.7\n        }\n    }\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        json.dump(config, f, indent=4)\n    return config\n\n# ---------------------- Explanatory Document Generator ---------------------------\n\ndef generate_explanatory_document(doc_path, wav_file, synth_data, config):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generates a Markdown document explaining the configuration.\n    \"\"\"\n    with open(doc_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Configuration Explanation\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"**Source Audio:** `{wav_file}`\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"## Audio Analysis\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"- **Fundamental Frequency:** {synth_data['fundamental_freq']:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"- **Detected MIDI Notes:** {synth_data['detected_notes']}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"- **Envelope (ADSR):**\\n\")\n        for k, v in synth_data['envelope'].items():\n            f.write(f\"  - {k.capitalize()}: {v:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"- **Spectral Centroid:** {synth_data['spectral_centroid']:.2f} Hz\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"## Synthesizer Configuration\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"",
                        "\"\"\"\nMIDI & Audio Optimization Toolkit\n\nThis script provides a suite of tools for:\n1. Optimizing Python scripts for MIDI input devices.\n2. Analyzing user-provided .WAV files to generate synthesizer data text files.\n3. Fine-tuning virtual instruments in a DAW (Digital Audio Workstation).\n4. Producing an explanatory document on the configurations.\n\nDependencies:\n- mido (for MIDI handling)\n- numpy, scipy (for audio analysis)\n- soundfile (for reading .wav files)\n- pretty_midi (for MIDI processing, optional)\n- python-rtmidi (for real-time MIDI, optional)\n\nInstall with:\npip install mido numpy scipy soundfile pretty_midi\n\nAuthor: [Your Name]\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport sys\nimport mido\nimport soundfile as sf\nimport numpy as np\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\nfrom scipy.fft import rfft, rfftfreq\nimport datetime\n\n# ----------- 1. MIDI Script Optimization -----------\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(script_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyzes and suggests optimizations for a Python MIDI input script.\n    Currently, it checks for:\n    - Inefficient polling loops\n    - Unused imports\n    - Suboptimal buffer handling\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Optimizing MIDI script: {script_path}\")\n    with open(script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    suggestions = []\n    for i, line in enumerate(lines):\n        if 'while True' in line and 'input.poll()' in ''.join(lines[i:i+5]):\n            suggestions.append(\n                f\"Line {i+1}: Consider using mido's iter_pending() or callback-based input instead of polling in a tight loop.\"\n            )\n        if 'import time' in line and 'time.sleep' not in ''.join(lines):\n            suggestions.append(\n                f\"Line {i+1}: 'import time' is unused.\"\n            )\n        if 'buffer' in line and 'size=' not in line:\n            suggestions.append(\n                f\"Line {i+1}: Consider specifying buffer size for efficient MIDI input.\"\n            )\n\n    if suggestions:\n        print(\"Optimization suggestions:\")\n        for s in suggestions:\n            print(\"  -\", s)\n    else:\n        print(\"No major inefficiencies detected.\")\n    return suggestions\n\n# ----------- 2. Analyze WAV & Generate Synth Data -----------\n\ndef analyze_wav(wav_path, output_txt_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyzes a .wav file to extract basic synthesizer parameters:\n    - Fundamental frequency (pitch)\n    - Amplitude envelope (ADSR estimation)\n    - Spectral centroid (timbre)\n    Outputs a text file with these parameters.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Analyzing WAV file: {wav_path}\")\n    data, sr = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if len(data.shape) > 1:  # Stereo to mono\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)\n    duration = len(data) / sr\n\n    # Estimate pitch (fundamental frequency) using FFT\n    N = len(data)\n    yf = np.abs(rfft(data))\n    xf = rfftfreq(N, 1 / sr)\n    peak_idx, _ = find_peaks(yf, height=np.max(yf)*0.1)\n    if len(peak_idx) == 0:\n        fundamental_freq = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental_freq = xf[peak_idx[0]]\n\n    # Amplitude envelope (simple ADSR estimation)\n    env = np.abs(data)\n    attack_time = np.argmax(env > 0.9 * np.max(env)) / sr\n    decay_time = np.argmax(env < 0.7 * np.max(env)) / sr - attack_time\n    sustain_level = np.mean(env[int(0.5*N):int(0.8*N)]) / np.max(env)\n    release_time = duration - np.argmax(env > 0.1 * np.max(env)) / sr\n\n    # Spectral centroid\n    spectral_centroid = np.sum(xf * yf) / np.sum(yf)\n\n    # Write synth data\n    with open(output_txt_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data Generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Sample Rate: {sr}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Duration: {duration:.2f} sec\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental Frequency: {fundamental_freq:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Attack Time: {attack_time:.3f} sec\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Decay Time: {decay_time:.3f} sec\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Sustain Level: {sustain_level:.2f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Release Time: {release_time:.3f} sec\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Spectral Centroid: {spectral_centroid:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n    print(f\"Synth data written to {output_txt_path}\")\n\n    return {\n        \"sample_rate\": sr,\n        \"duration\": duration,\n        \"fundamental_freq\": fundamental_freq,\n        \"attack_time\": attack_time,\n        \"decay_time\": decay_time,\n        \"sustain_level\": sustain_level,\n        \"release_time\": release_time,\n        \"spectral_centroid\": spectral_centroid\n    }\n\n# ----------- 3. Fine-tune Virtual Instruments -----------\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(synth_data, daw_config_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generates a DAW configuration file (text) for a virtual instrument,\n    based on analyzed synth data.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Generating DAW instrument config: {daw_config_path}\")\n    with open(daw_config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(\"# DAW Instrument Configuration\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Instrument Name: AutoSynth_{datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Oscillator Frequency: {synth_data['fundamental_freq']:.2f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope Attack: {synth_data['attack_time']:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope Decay: {synth_data['decay_time']:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope Sustain: {synth_data['sustain_level']:.2f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope Release: {synth_data['release_time']:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Spectral Centroid (Timbre): {synth_data['spectral_centroid']:.2f}\\n\")\n        f.write(\"Suggested DAW: Ableton, FL Studio, Logic Pro, Reaper\\n\")\n    print(f\"DAW config written to {daw_config_path}\")\n\n# ----------- 4. Explanatory Document Generation -----------\n\ndef generate_explanatory_doc(synth_data, daw_config_path, doc_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Produces an explanatory document describing the configuration and\n    how parameters were derived.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Writing explanatory document: {doc_path}\")\n    with open(doc_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(\"=== Synthesizer & DAW Configuration Explanation ===\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(\"This document explains the synthesizer parameters and DAW configuration generated from your .wav file.\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(\"1. Fundamental Frequency: The main pitch detected in the sample, used to set the oscillator frequency.\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"   Value: {synth_data['fundamental_freq']:.2f} Hz\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(\"2. Amplitude Envelope (ADSR):\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"   - Attack: {synth_data['attack_time']:.3f} sec (time to reach peak amplitude)\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"   - Decay: {synth_data['decay_time']:.3f} sec (time to drop to sustain level)\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"   - Sustain: {synth_data['sustain_level']:.2f} (level during main sequence)\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"   - Release: {synth_data['release_time']:.3f} sec (time to fade after note off)\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(\"3. Spectral Centroid: Indicates the brightness/timbre of the sound.\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"   Value: {synth_data['spectral_centroid']:.2f} Hz\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(\"4. DAW Configuration:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"   See generated config file: {daw_config_path}\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(\"You can load these parameters into a virtual instrument (e.g., Ableton's Operator, FL Studio's 3xOSC) for a similar sound.\\n\")\n    print(f\"Explanatory document written to {doc_path}\")\n\n# ----------- Main CLI -----------\n\ndef main():\n    import argparse\n\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description=\"MIDI & Audio Optimization Toolkit\")\n    parser.add_argument('--optimize-midi', type=str, help=\"Path to Python script for MIDI input optimization.\")\n    parser.add_argument('--analyze-wav', type=str, help=\"Path to .wav file to analyze.\")\n    parser.add_argument('--output-prefix', type=str, default=\"output\", help=\"Prefix for generated files.\")\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    if args.optimize_midi:\n        optimize_midi_script(args.optimize_midi)\n\n    if args.analyze_wav:\n        synth_txt = f\"{args.output_prefix}_synth.txt\"\n        daw_cfg = f\"{args.output_prefix}_daw_config.txt\"\n        doc_txt = f\"{args.output_prefix}_explanation.txt\"\n        synth_data = analyze_wav(args.analyze_wav, synth_txt)\n        fine_tune_instrument(synth_data, daw_cfg)\n        generate_explanatory_doc(synth_data, daw_cfg, doc_txt)\n\n    if not args.optimize_midi and not args.analyze_wav:\n        parser.print_help()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()"

                        "import unittest\nimport tempfile\nimport os\nimport shutil\nimport numpy as np\nimport mido\nimport soundfile as sf\n\n# Import functions from the provided code\n# For this test script, we assume the functions are accessible in the same namespace.\n# If they are in a module, you would use: from <module> import <function>\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# Copy-pasted functions from the code to enable testing in this script\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write('\\n'.join(optimized_lines))\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    # Envelope extraction (simple method)\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024)/1024, mode='same')\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * np.max(env))\n    decay_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.8 * np.max(env))\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * np.max(env)) - 1\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else np.max(env)\n\n    # Fundamental frequency detection (FFT peak)\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    from scipy.signal import find_peaks\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    # Harmonics\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag)))\n\n    # Save to text file\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx-attack_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {(len(env)-release_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Harmonics:\\n\")\n        for i, (freq_h, mag_h) in enumerate(harmonics, 1):\n            f.write(f\"  Harmonic_{i}: {freq_h:.2f} Hz, {mag_h:.3f} (relative)\\n\")\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(config_path, tuning_cents=0):\n    if not os.path.exists(config_path):\n        return\n    with open(config_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    new_lines = []\n    found = False\n    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n\ndef generate_explanatory_doc(output_path, midi_scripts, wav_files, synth_data_files, instrument_configs):\n    with open(output_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# MIDI & Synthesizer Configuration Summary\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Generated on {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"## Optimized MIDI Scripts\\n\")\n        for script in midi_scripts:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(script)}: Optimized for redundant CC removal and event merging.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Synthesizer Data Files\\n\")\n        for wav, synth in zip(wav_files, synth_data_files):\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(synth)}: Generated from {os.path.basename(wav)} with analyzed pitch, envelope, and harmonics.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Virtual Instrument Configurations\\n\")\n        for config in instrument_configs:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(config)}: Fine-tuned for cent-level pitch adjustment.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n---\\n\")\n        f.write(\"### Notes\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- MIDI scripts are optimized for efficiency and minimal latency.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Synthesizer data files can be imported into most additive/subtractive synths.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Instrument configuration files should be loaded into your DAW's virtual instrument plugin.\\n\")\n\nclass TestMidiAudioToolkit(unittest.TestCase):\n    def                     "agent": "Test Executor",
                    "best_code": "\"\"\"\nMIDI & Audio Optimization Toolkit\n\nThis script provides three main functionalities:\n1. Optimize MIDI input device scripts.\n2. Analyze .wav files to generate synthesizer data text files.\n3. Fine-tune virtual instruments in a DAW (Digital Audio Workstation) via configuration files.\n4. Generate an explanatory document summarizing configurations.\n\nRequirements:\n- mido (for MIDI handling)\n- numpy, scipy (for audio analysis)\n- soundfile (for reading .wav files)\n- python-rtmidi (optional, for advanced MIDI I/O)\n\nInstall dependencies via pip if necessary:\npip install mido numpy scipy soundfile\n\nAuthor: [Your Name]\nDate: 2024-06\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport sys\nimport glob\nimport mido\nimport numpy as np\nimport soundfile as sf\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# ----------------------------- MIDI Script Optimizer -----------------------------\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Optimize an existing MIDI script by removing redundant CC messages and merging similar events.\n    Assumes the script is a text file with one MIDI message per line in mido format.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Optimizing MIDI script: {midi_script_path}\")\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write('\\n'.join(optimized_lines))\n    print(f\"Optimized script saved to: {optimized_script_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- WAV Analyzer & Synth Data Generator -----------------------------\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze a .wav file and generate a synthesizer data text file containing:\n    - Detected fundamental frequency (pitch)\n    - Envelope (attack, decay, sustain, release)\n    - Main harmonics (for additive synthesis)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Analyzing WAV file: {wav_path}\")\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    # Envelope extraction (simple method)\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024)/1024, mode='same')\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * np.max(env))\n    decay_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.8 * np.max(env))\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * np.max(env)) - 1\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else np.max(env)\n\n    # Fundamental frequency detection (FFT peak)\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    # Harmonics\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag)))\n\n    # Save to text file\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx-attack_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release:                         "\"\"\"\nMIDI & Audio Optimization Toolkit\n\nThis script provides four main functionalities:\n1. Optimize MIDI input device scripts.\n2. Analyze .wav files to generate synthesizer data text files.\n3. Fine-tune virtual instruments in a DAW via configuration files.\n4. Generate an explanatory document summarizing configurations.\n\nRequirements:\n- mido (for MIDI handling)\n- numpy, scipy (for audio analysis)\n- soundfile (for reading .wav files)\n\nInstall dependencies via pip if necessary:\npip install mido numpy scipy soundfile\n\nAuthor: [Your Name]\nDate: 2024-06\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport sys\nimport mido\nimport numpy as np\nimport soundfile as sf\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# ----------------------------- MIDI Script Optimizer -----------------------------\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Optimize an existing MIDI script by removing redundant CC messages and merging similar events.\n    Assumes the script is a text file with one MIDI message per line in mido format.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Optimizing MIDI script: {midi_script_path}\")\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write('\\n'.join(optimized_lines))\n    print(f\"Optimized script saved to: {optimized_script_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- WAV Analyzer & Synth Data Generator -----------------------------\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze a .wav file and generate a synthesizer data text file containing:\n    - Detected fundamental frequency (pitch)\n    - Envelope (attack, decay, sustain, release)\n    - Main harmonics (for additive synthesis)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Analyzing WAV file: {wav_path}\")\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    # Envelope extraction (moving average)\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024)/1024, mode='same')\n    max_env = np.max(env)\n    # Attack: time to reach 5% of max\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * max_env)\n    # Decay: time to reach 80% of max after attack\n    decay_idx = attack_idx + np.argmax(env[attack_idx:] > 0.8 * max_env)\n    # Release: time from end where env drops below 5% of max\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * max_env) - 1\n    # Sustain: max level between decay and release\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else max_env\n\n    # Fundamental frequency detection (FFT peak)\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    # Harmonics\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag) if np.max(mag) else 0))\n\n    # Save to text file\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx-attack_idx)/samplerate:.3f} ----------------------------- Virtual Instrument Fine-Tuner -----------------------------\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(config_path, tuning_cents=0):\n    \"\"\"\n    Fine-tune a virtual instrument by os.path.exists(config_path):\n        print(\"Config file not found.\")\n        return\n    with open(config_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    new_lines = []\n    found = False\n    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n    print(f\"Instrument fine-tuned by {tuning_cents} cents.\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Explanatory Document Generator -----------------------------\n\ndef generate_explanatory_doc(output_path, {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"## Optimized MIDI Scripts\\n\")\n        for script in midi_scripts:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(script)}:                         "\"\"\"\nMIDI & Audio Optimization Toolkit\n\nThis script provides four main functionalities:\n1. Optimize MIDI input device scripts.\n2. Analyze .wav files to generate synthesizer data text files.\n3. Fine-tune virtual instruments in a DAW via configuration files.\n4. Generate an explanatory document summarizing configurations.\n\nRequirements:\n- mido (for MIDI handling)\n- numpy, scipy (for audio analysis)\n- soundfile (for reading .wav files)\n\nInstall dependencies via pip:\n    pip install mido numpy scipy soundfile\n\nAuthor: [Your Name]\nDate: 2024-06\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport sys\nimport mido\nimport numpy as np\nimport soundfile as sf\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# ----------------------------- MIDI Script Optimizer -----------------------------\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Optimize an existing MIDI script by removing redundant CC messages and merging similar events.\n    Assumes the script is a text file with one MIDI message per line in mido format.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"[MIDI OPTIMIZER] Processing: {midi_script_path}\")\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}  # (channel, control): value\n    last_note = {}  # (channel, note): velocity\n\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n\n        # Merge consecutive identical note_on events (velocity unchanged)\n        if msg.type == 'note_on' and msg.velocity > 0:\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.note)\n            if key in last_note and last_note[key] == msg.velocity:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_note[key] = msg.velocity\n\n        # Remove redundant note_off events (if previous note_off for same note)\n        if msg.type == 'note_off':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.note)\n            if key in last_note and last_note[key] == 0:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_note[key] = 0\n\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write('\\n'.join(optimized_lines))\n    print(f\"[MIDI OPTIMIZER] Optimized script saved to: {optimized_script_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- WAV Analyzer & Synth Data Generator -----------------------------\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze a .wav file and generate a synthesizer data text file containing:\n    - Detected fundamental frequency (pitch)\n    - Envelope (attack, decay, sustain, release)\n    - Main harmonics (for additive synthesis)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"[WAV ANALYZER] Processing: {wav_path}\")\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    # Envelope extraction (moving average)\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    window_size = int(0.02 * samplerate)  # 20ms window\n    if window_size < 1:\n        window_size = 1\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(window_size)/window_size, mode='same')\n\n    # Attack: time to reach 10% max, Decay: time to reach sustain, Release: from sustain to silence\n    max_env = np.max(env)\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.1 * max_env)\n    decay_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.7 * max_env)\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.1 * max_env) - 1\n    sustain_level = np.mean(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else max_env\n\n    # Fundamental frequency detection (FFT peak)\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    # Ignore DC\n    mag[0] = 0\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        # Find lowest peak above 20 Hz\n        valid_peaks = [p for p in peaks if freq[p] > 20]\n        fundamental = freq[valid_peaks[0]] if valid_peaks else freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    # Harmonics\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag)))\n\n    # Save to text file\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx-attack_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {(len(env)-release_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Harmonics:\\n\")\n        for i, (freq_h, mag_h) in enumerate(harmonics, 1):\n            f.write(f\"  Harmonic_{i}: {freq_h:.2f} Hz, {mag_h:.3f} (relative)\\n\")\n    print(f\"[WAV ANALYZER] Synthesizer data saved to: {synth_data_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Virtual Instrument Fine-Tuner -----------------------------\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(config_path, tuning_cents=0):\n    \"\"\"\n    Fine-tune a virtual instrument by updating its configuration file.\n    Assumes the config file is a simple key=value text file.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"[INSTRUMENT TUNER] Processing: {config_path}\")\n    if not os.path.exists(config_path):\n        print(\"[INSTRUMENT TUNER] Config file not found.\")\n        return\n    with open(config_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    new_lines = []\n    found = False\n    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n    print(f\"[INSTRUMENT TUNER] Instrument fine-tuned by {tuning_cents} cents.\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Explanatory Document Generator -----------------------------\n\ndef generate_explanatory_doc(output_path, midi_scripts, wav_files, synth_data_files, instrument_configs):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generate a markdown document explaining the configurations and processing.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"[DOC GENERATOR] Generating: {output_path}\")\n    with open(output_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# MIDI & Synthesizer Configuration Summary\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Generated on {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\\n\\n\")\n\n        f.write(f\"## Optimized MIDI Scripts\\n\")\n        for script in midi_scripts:\n            f.write(f\"- `{os.path.basename(script)}`: Optimized for redundant CC removal and event merging.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Synthesizer Data Files\\n\")\n        for wav, synth in zip(wav_files, synth_data_files):\n            f.write(f\"- `{os.path.basename(synth)}`: Generated from `{os.path.basename(wav)}` with analyzed pitch, envelope, and harmonics.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Virtual Instrument Configurations\\n\")\n        for config in instrument_configs:\n            f.write(f\"- `{os.path.basename(config)}`: Fine-tuned for cent-level pitch adjustment.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n---\\n\")\n        f.write(\"### Notes\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- MIDI scripts are optimized for efficiency and minimal latency.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Synthesizer data files can be imported into most additive/subtractive synths.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Instrument configuration files should be loaded into your DAW's virtual instrument plugin.\\n\")\n    print(f\"[DOC GENERATOR] Document saved to: {output_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Main CLI Interface -----------------------------\n\ndef main():\n    import argparse\n\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description=\"MIDI & Audio Optimization Toolkit\",\n        epilog=\"Examples:\\n\"\n               \"  python script.py --optimize-midi input.txt optimized.txt\\n\"\n               \"  python                         "\"\"\"\nMIDI & Audio Optimization Toolkit\n\nThis script provides four main functionalities:\n1. np\nimport soundfile as sf\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# ----------------------------- MIDI Script Optimizer -----------------------------\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Optimize a MIDI script by removing redundant control change (CC) messages and merging similar events.\n    Assumes the script is a text file with one MIDI message per line in mido string format.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Optimizing MIDI script: {midi_script_path}\")\n    if not os.path.exists(midi_script_path):\n        print(f\"Error: MIDI script '{midi_script_path}' not found.\")\n        return\n\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}  # (channel, control): value\n\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            # If the line can't be parsed, keep it as is\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if last_cc.get(key) == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n -----------------------------\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze a .wav file and generate a synthesizer data text file containing:\n    - Detected fundamental frequency (pitch)\n    - Envelope (attack, decay, sustain, release)\n    - Main harmonics (for additive synthesis)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Analyzing WAV file: {wav_path}\")\n    if not os.path.exists(wav_path):\n        print(f\"Error: WAV file '{wav_path}' not found.\")\n        return\n\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    # Envelope extraction (simple moving average)\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024) / 1024, mode='same')\n\n    # Attack: first time envelope rises above 5% of max\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * np.max(env))\n    # Decay: first time after attack envelope drops below 80% of max\n    decay_idx = attack_idx + np.argmax(env[attack_idx:] < 0.8 * np.max(env))\n    # Release: last time envelope drops below 5% of max\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] < 0.05 * np.max(env)) - 1\n    # Sustain: max between decay and release\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else np.max(env)\n\n    # Fundamental frequency detection (FFT peak)\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1 / samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag) * 0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0.0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    # Harmonics: find up to num_harmonics multiples of the fundamental\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics + 1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx] / np.max(mag)))\n\n    # Save to text file\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx / samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx - attack_idx) / samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {(len(env) - release_idx) / samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(\"Harmonics:\\n\")\n        for i, (freq_h, mag_h) in enumerate(harmonics, 1):\n            f.write(f\"  Harmonic_{i}: {freq_h:.2f} Hz, {mag_h:.3f} (relative)\\n\")\n    print(f\"Synthesizer data saved to: {synth_data_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Virtual Instrument Fine-Tuner -----------------------------\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(config_path, tuning_cents=0):\n    \"\"\"\n    Fine-tune a virtual instrument by updating its configuration file.\n    Assumes the config file is a simple key=value text file.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Fine-tuning instrument config: {config_path}\")\n    if not os.path.exists(config_path):\n        print(f\"Error: Config file '{config_path}' not found.\")\n        return\n\n    with open(config_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    new_lines = []\n    found = False\n    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n    print(f\"Instrument fine-tuned by {tuning_cents} cents.\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Explanatory Document Generator -----------------------------\n\ndef                         "import os\nimport tempfile\nimport shutil\nimport unittest\nimport numpy as np\n\n# Mock mido for tests if not installed\ntry:\n    import mido\nexcept ImportError:\n    import sys\n    import types\n    mido = types.SimpleNamespace()\n    class Message:\n        def __init__(self, type, channel=0, control=0, value=0):\n            self.type = type\n            self.channel = channel\n            self.control = control\n            self.value = value\n        @classmethod\n        def from_str(cls, s):\n            # Only handles control_change messages for test\n            if s.startswith('control_change'):\n                # e.g. control_change channel=0 control=1 value=64\n                parts = s.split()\n                args = {k: int(v) for k, v in [p.split('=') for p in parts[1:]]}\n                return cls('control_change', **args)\n            raise ValueError(\"Unknown message\")\n        def __str__(self):\n            return f'control_change channel={self.channel} control={self.control} value={self.value}'\n    mido.Message = Message\n\nimport soundfile as sf\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\n\n# Import functions from the code to test\n# (In a real test, these would be imported from the module, but here we redefine them.)\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write('\\n'.join(optimized_lines))\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024)/1024, mode='same')\n    max_env = np.max(env)\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * max_env)\n    decay_idx = attack_idx + np.argmax(env[attack_idx:] > 0.8 * max_env)\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * max_env) - 1\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else max_env\n\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag) if np.max(mag) else 0))\n\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx-attack_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {(len(env)-release_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Harmonics:\\n\")\n        for i, (freq_h, mag_h) in enumerate(harmonics, 1):\n            f.write(f\"  Harmonic_{i}: {freq_h:.2f} Hz, {mag_h:.3f} (relative)\\n\")\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(config_path, tuning_cents=0):\n    if not os.path.exists(config_path):\n        return\n    with open(config_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    new_lines = []\n    found = False\n    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n\ndef generate_explanatory_doc(output_path, midi_scripts, wav_files, optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write('\\n'.join(optimized_lines))\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024)/1024, mode='same')\n    max_env = np.max(env)\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * max_env)\n    decay_idx = attack_idx + np.argmax(env[attack_idx:] > 0.8 * max_env)\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * max_env) - 1\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else max_env\n\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    from scipy.signal import find_peaks\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag) if np.max(mag) else 0))\n\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx-attack_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {(len(env)-release_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Harmonics:\\n\")\n        for i, (freq_h, mag_h) in enumerate(harmonics, 1):\n            f.write(f\"  Harmonic_{i}: {freq_h:.2f} Hz, {mag_h:.3f} (relative)\\n\")\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(config_path, tuning_cents=0):\n    if not os.path.exists(config_path):\n        return\n    with open(config_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    new_lines = []\n    found = False\n    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n\ndef generate_explanatory_doc(output_path, midi_scripts, wav_files, synth_data_files, instrument_configs):\n    from datetime import datetime\n    with open(output_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# MIDI & Synthesizer Configuration Summary\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Generated on {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"## Optimized MIDI Scripts\\n\")\n        for script in midi_scripts:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(script)}: Optimized for redundant CC removal and event merging.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Synthesizer Data Files\\n\")\n        for wav, synth in zip(wav_files, synth_data_files):\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(synth)}: Generated from {os.path.basename(wav)} with analyzed pitch, envelope, and harmonics.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Virtual Instrument Configurations\\n\")\n        for config in instrument_configs:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(config)}: Fine-tuned for cent-level pitch adjustment.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n---\\n\")\n        f.write(\"### Notes\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- MIDI scripts are optimized for efficiency and minimal latency.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Synthesizer data files can be imported into most additive/subtractive synths.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Instrument configuration files should be loaded into your DAW's virtual instrument plugin.\\n\")\n\n# --- Test Suite sf\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# ----------------------------- MIDI Script Optimizer -----------------------------\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Optimize an existing MIDI script by removing redundant CC messages and merging similar events.\n    Assumes the script is a text file with one MIDI message per line in mido format.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Optimizing MIDI script: {midi_script_path}\")\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write('\\n'.join(optimized_lines))\n    print(f\"Optimized script saved to: {optimized_script_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- WAV Analyzer & Synth Data Generator -----------------------------\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze a .wav file and generate a synthesizer data text file containing:\n    - Detected fundamental frequency (pitch)\n    - Envelope (attack, decay, sustain, release)\n    - Main harmonics (for additive synthesis)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Analyzing WAV file: {wav_path}\")\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    # Envelope extraction (moving average)\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024)/1024, mode='same')\n    max_env = np.max(env)\n    # Attack: time to reach 5% of max\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * max_env)\n    # Decay: time to reach 80% of max after attack\n    decay_idx = attack_idx + np.argmax(env[attack_idx:] > 0.8 * max_env)\n    # Release: time from end where env drops below 5% of max\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * max_env) - 1\n    # Sustain: max level between decay and release\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else max_env\n\n    # Fundamental frequency detection (FFT peak)\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    # Harmonics\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag) if np.max(mag) else 0))\n\n    # Save to text file\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx-attack_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {(len(env)-release_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Harmonics:\\n\")\n        for i, (freq_h, mag_h) in enumerate(harmonics, 1):\n            f.write(f\"  Harmonic_{i}: {freq_h:.2f} Hz, {mag_h:.3f} (relative)\\n\")\n    print(f\"Synthesizer data saved to: {synth_data_path}\")\n\n#    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n Optimized for redundant CC removal and event merging.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Synthesizer Data Files\\n\")\n        for wav, synth in zip(wav_files, synth_data_files):\n            f.write(f\"- sf\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# ----------------------------- MIDI Script Optimizer -----------------------------\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Optimize an existing MIDI script by removing redundant CC messages and merging similar events.\n    Assumes the script is a text file with one MIDI message per line in mido format.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Optimizing MIDI script: {midi_script_path}\")\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as -----------------------------\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze a .wav file and generate a synthesizer data text file containing:\n    - Detected fundamental frequency (pitch)\n    - Envelope (attack, decay, sustain, release)\n    - Main harmonics (for additive synthesis)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Analyzing WAV file: {wav_path}\")\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    # Envelope extraction (moving average)\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024)/1024, mode='same')\n    max_env = np.max(env)\n    # Attack: time to reach 5% of max\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * max_env)\n    # Decay: time to reach 80% of max after attack\n    decay_idx = attack_idx + np.argmax(env[attack_idx:] > 0.8 * max_env)\n    # Release: time from end where env drops below 5% of max\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * max_env) - 1\n    # Sustain: max level between decay and release\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else max_env\n\n    # Fundamental frequency detection (FFT peak)\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    # Harmonics\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag) if np.max(mag) else 0))\n\n    # Save to text file\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {(len(env)-release_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Harmonics:\\n\")\n        for i, (freq_h, mag_h) in enumerate(harmonics, 1):\n            f.write(f\"  Harmonic_{i}: {freq_h:.2f} Hz, {mag_h:.3f} (relative)\\n\")\n    print(f\"Synthesizer data saved to: {synth_data_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Virtual Instrument Fine-Tuner -----------------------------\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(config_path, tuning_cents=0):\n    \"\"\"\n    Fine-tune a virtual instrument by    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"## Optimized MIDI Scripts\\n\")\n        for script in midi_scripts:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(script)}: Optimized for redundant CC removal and event merging.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Synthesizer Data Files\\n\")\n        for wav, synth in zip(wav_files, synth_data_files):\n            f.write(f\"-                         "\"\"\"\nMIDI & Audio Optimization Toolkit\n\nThis script provides four main functionalities:\n1. Optimize MIDI input device scripts.\n2. Analyze .wav files to generate synthesizer data text files.\n3. Fine-tune virtual instruments in a DAW via configuration files.\n4. Generate an explanatory document summarizing configurations.\n\nRequirements:\n- mido (for MIDI handling)\n- numpy, scipy (for audio analysis)\n- soundfile (for reading .wav files)\n\nInstall dependencies via pip if necessary:\npip install mido numpy scipy soundfile\n\nAuthor: [Your Name]\nDate: 2024-06\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport sys\nimport mido\nimport numpy as np\nimport soundfile as sf\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\n# ----------------------------- MIDI Script Optimizer -----------------------------\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Optimize an existing MIDI script by removing redundant CC messages and merging similar events.\n    Assumes the script is a text file with one MIDI message per line in mido format.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Optimizing MIDI script: {midi_script_path}\")\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}  # Track last value for each CC per channel\n\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write('\\n'.join(optimized_lines))\n    print(f\"Optimized script saved to: {optimized_script_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- WAV Analyzer & Synth Data Generator -----------------------------\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze a .wav file and generate a synthesizer data text file containing:\n    - Detected fundamental frequency (pitch)\n    - Envelope (attack, decay, sustain, release)\n    - Main harmonics (for additive synthesis)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Analyzing WAV file: {wav_path}\")\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    # Envelope extraction (moving average)\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    window_size = min(1024, len(abs_data)//10)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(window_size)/window_size, mode='same')\n    max_env = np.max(env)\n    # Attack: time to reach 5% of max\n    try:\n        attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * max_env)\n    except Exception:\n        attack_idx = 0\n    # Decay: time to reach 80% of max after attack\n    try:\n        decay_idx = attack_idx + np.argmax(env[attack_idx:] > 0.8 * max_env)\n    except Exception:\n        decay_idx = attack_idx\n    # Release: time from end where env drops below 5% of max\n    try:\n        release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * max_env) - 1\n    except Exception:\n        release_idx = len(env) - 1\n    # Sustain: max level between decay and release\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else max_env\n\n    # Fundamental frequency detection (FFT peak)\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    fundamental = 0.0\n    if len(peaks) > 0:\n        # Try to find the lowest peak above 20Hz (avoid DC offset)\n        valid_peaks = [p for p in peaks if freq[p] > 20]\n        if valid_peaks:\n            fundamental = freq[valid_peaks[0]]\n        else:\n            fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    # Harmonics\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        if target_freq > freq[-1]:\n            harmonics.append((target_freq, 0.0))\n            continue\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag) if np.max(mag) else 0))\n\n    # Save to text file\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx-attack_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {(len(env)-release_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Harmonics:\\n\")\n        for i, (freq_h, mag_h) in enumerate(harmonics, 1):\n            f.write(f\"  Harmonic_{i}: {freq_h:.2f} Hz, {mag_h:.3f} (relative)\\n\")\n    print(f\"Synthesizer data saved to: {synth_data_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Virtual Instrument Fine-Tuner -----------------------------\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(config_path, tuning_cents=0):\n    \"\"\"\n    Fine-tune a virtual instrument by updating its configuration file.\n    Assumes the config file is a simple key=value text file.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Fine-tuning instrument config: {config_path}\")\n    if not os.path.exists(config_path):\n        print(\"Config file not found.\")\n        return\n    with open(config_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    new_lines = []\n    found = False\n    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n    print(f\"Instrument fine-tuned by {tuning_cents} cents.\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Explanatory Document Generator -----------------------------\n\ndef generate_explanatory_doc(output_path, midi_scripts, wav_files, synth_data_files, instrument_configs):\n    \"\"\"\n    Generate a markdown document explaining the configurations and processing.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Generating explanatory document: {output_path}\")\n    with open(output_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# MIDI & Synthesizer Configuration Summary\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Generated on {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"## Optimized MIDI Scripts\\n\")\n        for script in midi_scripts:\n            f.write(f\"- **{os.path.basename(script)}**: Optimized for redundant CC removal and event merging.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Synthesizer Data Files\\n\")\n        for wav, synth in zip(wav_files, synth_data_files):\n            f.write(f\"- **{os.path.basename(synth)}**: Generated from *{os.path.basename(wav)}* with analyzed pitch, envelope, and harmonics.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Virtual Instrument Configurations\\n\")\n        for config in instrument_configs:\n            f.write(f\"- **{os.path.basename(config)}**: Fine-tuned for cent-level pitch adjustment.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n---\\n\")\n        f.write(\"### Notes\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- MIDI scripts are file\n        for config in instrument_configs:\n            f.write(f\"\\n#### {os.path.basename(config)}\\n\")\n            if os.path.exists(config):\n                with open(config, 'r') as                         "import os\nimport tempfile\nimport shutil\nimport unittest\nimport io\nimport sys\n\nimport numpy as np\n\n# Patch sys.argv for main() testing if needed\n# Import the functions to test from the user code\nimport mido\nimport soundfile as sf\n\n# The functions to test (copy-pasted from user code, but in real use, import from the module)\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\n\n# Copy the functions here for test context (in real use, import from the module)\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write('\\n'.join(optimized_lines))\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024)/1024, mode='same')\n    max_env = np.max(env)\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * max_env)\n    decay_idx = attack_idx + np.argmax(env[attack_idx:] > 0.8 * max_env)\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * max_env) - 1\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else max_env\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag) if np.max(mag) else 0))\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx-attack_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {(len(env)-release_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Harmonics:\\n\")\n        for i, (freq_h, mag_h) in enumerate(harmonics, 1):\n            f.write(f\"  Harmonic_{i}: {freq_h:.2f} Hz, {mag_h:.3f} (relative)\\n\")\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(config_path, tuning_cents=0):\n    if not os.path.exists(config_path):\n        return\n    with open(config_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n    new_lines = []\n    found = False\n    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n\ndef generate_explanatory_doc(output_path, midi_scripts, wav_files, synth_data_files, instrument_configs):\n    with open(output_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# MIDI & Synthesizer Configuration Summary\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Generated on {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"## Optimized MIDI Scripts\\n\")\n        for script in midi_scripts:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(script)}: Optimized for redundant CC removal and event merging.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Synthesizer Data Files\\n\")\n        for wav, synth in zip(wav_files, synth_data_files):\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(synth)}: Generated from {os.path.basename(wav)} with analyzed pitch, envelope, and harmonics.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Virtual Instrument Configurations\\n\")\n        for config in instrument_configs:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(config)}: Fine-tuned for cent-level pitch adjustment.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n---\\n\")\n        f.write(\"### Notes\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- MIDI scripts are optimized for efficiency and minimal latency.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Synthesizer data files can be imported into most additive/subtractive synths.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Instrument configuration files should be loaded into your DAW's virtual instrument plugin.\\n\")\n\nclass TestMidiAudioToolkit(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.test_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()\n        self.addCleanup(shutil.rmtree, self.test_dir)\n\n    # ------------------ Tests for optimize_midi_script ------------------\n\n    def                         "import unittest\nimport tempfile\nimport os\nimport shutil\nimport numpy as np\n\n# Patch sys.argv so main() doesn't parse CLI during import\nimport sys\nsys.argv = [sys.argv[0]]\n\n# Import the code under test (assume it's in the same file for this test suite)\n# If the code is in another file, use: from <filename> import <functions>\nfrom io import StringIO\n\nimport mido\nimport soundfile as sf\n\n# Re-import functions from the code under test\nfrom __main__ import (\n    optimize_midi_script,\n    analyze_wav_to_synth_data,\n    fine_tune_instrument,\n    generate_explanatory_doc,\n)\n\nclass TestMidiAudioToolkit(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # Create a temp directory for all file operations\n        self.test_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()\n    \n    def tearDown(self):\n        shutil.rmtree(self.test_dir)\n\n    # ---------- MIDI Script Optimizer Tests ----------\n    def test_optimize_midi_script_removes_redundant_cc(self):\n        midi_script = [\n            \"control_change channel=0 control=7 value=100\",\n            \"control_change channel=0 control=7 value=100\",  # redundant\n            \"control_change channel=0 control=7 value=101\",  # not redundant\n            \"note_on channel=0 note=60 velocity=64\",\n            \"# this is a comment\",\n            \"\",\n            \"control_change channel=0 control=10 value=50\",\n            \"control_change channel=0 control=10 value=50\",  # redundant\n        ]\n        input_path = os.path.join(self.test_dir, \"input_midi.txt\")\n        output_path = os.path.join(self.test_dir, \"output_midi.txt\")\n        with open(input_path, \"w\") as f:\n            f.write('\\n'.join(midi_script))\n        optimize_midi_script(input_path, output_path)\n        with open(output_path, \"r\") as f:\n            lines = [line.strip() for line in f.readlines()]\n        #
