Envelope values present\n        self.assertIn(\"Envelope:\", contents)\n        self.assertIn(\"Attack:\", contents)\n        self.assertIn(\"Decay:\", contents)\n        self.assertIn(\"Sustain_Level:\", contents)\n        self.assertIn(\"Release:\", contents)\n        #                         "import os\nimport tempfile\nimport shutil\nimport unittest\nimport numpy as np\n\n# Import the functions to test from the provided code.\n# For the test suite, we must copy the functions here directly since the code is not in a module.\n\nimport mido\nimport soundfile as sf\n\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\n\n# ----------------------------- MIDI Script Optimizer -----------------------------\n\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    print(f\"Optimizing MIDI script: {midi_script_path}\")\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write('\\n'.join(optimized_lines))\n    print(f\"Optimized script saved to: {optimized_script_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- WAV Analyzer & Synth Data Generator -----------------------------\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    print(f\"Analyzing WAV file: {wav_path}\")\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    # Envelope extraction (moving average)\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024)/1024, mode='same')\n    max_env = np.max(env)\n    # Attack: time to reach 5% of max\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * max_env)\n    # Decay: time to reach 80% of max after attack\n    decay_idx = attack_idx + np.argmax(env[attack_idx:] > 0.8 * max_env)\n    # Release: time from end where env drops below 5% of max\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * max_env) - 1\n    # Sustain: max level between decay and release\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else max_env\n\n    # Fundamental frequency detection (FFT peak)\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    # Harmonics\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag) if np.max(mag) else 0))\n\n    # Save to text file\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx-attack_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {(len(env)-release_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Harmonics:\\n\")\n        for i, (freq_h, mag_h) in enumerate(harmonics, 1):\n            f.write(f\"  Harmonic_{i}: {freq_h:.2f} Hz, {mag_h:.3f} (relative)\\n\")\n    print(f\"Synthesizer data saved to: {synth_data_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Virtual Instrument Fine-Tuner -----------------------------\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(config_path, tuning_cents=0):\n    print(f\"Fine-tuning instrument config: {config_path}\")\n    if not os.path.exists(config_path):\n        print(\"Config file not found.\")\n        return\n    with open(config_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    new_lines = []\n    found = False\n    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n    print(f\"Instrument fine-tuned by {tuning_cents} cents.\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Explanatory Document Generator -----------------------------\n\ndef generate_explanatory_doc(output_path, midi_scripts, wav_files, synth_data_files, instrument_configs):\n    print(f\"Generating explanatory document: {output_path}\")\n    with open(output_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# MIDI & Synthesizer Configuration Summary\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Generated on {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"## Optimized MIDI Scripts\\n\")\n        for script in midi_scripts:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(script)}: Optimized for redundant CC removal and event merging.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Synthesizer Data Files\\n\")\n        for wav, synth in zip(wav_files, synth_data_files):\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(synth)}: Generated from {os.path.basename(wav)} with analyzed pitch, envelope, and harmonics.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Virtual Instrument Configurations\\n\")\n        for config in instrument_configs:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(config)}: Fine-tuned for cent-level pitch adjustment.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n---\\n\")\n        f.write(\"### Notes\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- MIDI scripts are optimized for efficiency and minimal latency.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Synthesizer data files can be imported into most additive/subtractive synths.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Instrument configuration files should be loaded into your DAW's virtual instrument plugin.\\n\")\n    print(f\"Explanatory document saved to: {output_path}\")\n\n# ----------------------------- Test Suite -----------------------------\n\nclass TestMidiAudioToolkit(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        # with open(out_path, 'r') as f:\n            result = [line.strip() for line in f.readlines()]\n\n        # Redundant CC messages should be removed, comments and invalid lines preserved\n        expected = [\n            \"# This is a comment\",\n            \"\",\n            \"control_change channel=0 control=7 value=100\",\n            \"control_change channel=0 control=7 value=101\",\n            \"note_on channel=0 note=60 velocity=100\",\n            \"note_off channel=0 note=60 velocity=0\",\n            \"control_change channel=0 control=10 value=64\",\n            \"control_change as sf\n\nfrom scipy.signal import find_peaks\n\n# The functions to test (copied from the user code)\ndef optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as optimize_midi_script(midi_script_path, optimized_script_path):\n    \"\"\"\n    Optimize an existing MIDI script by removing redundant CC messages and merging similar events.\n    Assumes the script is a text file with one MIDI message per line in mido format.\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Optimizing MIDI script: {midi_script_path}\")\n    with open(midi_script_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    optimized_lines = []\n    last_cc = {}\n    for line in lines:\n        line = line.strip()\n        if not line or line.startswith('#'):\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        try:\n            msg = mido.Message.from_str(line)\n        except Exception:\n            optimized_lines.append(line)\n            continue\n        # Remove redundant CC messages (same control and value)\n        if msg.type == 'control_change':\n            key = (msg.channel, msg.control)\n            if key in last_cc and last_cc[key] == msg.value:\n                continue  # skip redundant\n            last_cc[key] = msg.value\n        optimized_lines.append(str(msg))\n\n    with open(optimized_script_path, 'w') as -----------------------------\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze a .wav file and generate a synthesizer data text file containing:\n    - Detected fundamental frequency (pitch)\n    - Envelope (attack, decay, sustain, release)\n    - Main harmonics (for additive synthesis)\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"Analyzing WAV file: {wav_path}\")\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    # Envelope extraction (moving average)\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024)/1024, mode='same')\n    max_env = np.max(env)\n    # Attack: time to reach 5% of max\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * max_env)\n    # Decay: time to reach 80% of max after attack\n    decay_idx = attack_idx + np.argmax(env[attack_idx:] > 0.8 * max_env)\n    # Release: time from end where env drops below 5% of max\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * max_env) - 1\n    # Sustain: max level between decay and release\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else max_env\n\n    # Fundamental frequency detection (FFT peak)\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    # Harmonics\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, f:\n        f.write('\\n'.join(optimized_lines))\n\ndef analyze_wav_to_synth_data(wav_path, synth_data_path, num_harmonics=8):\n    data, samplerate = sf.read(wav_path)\n    if data.ndim > 1:\n        data = np.mean(data, axis=1)  # Convert to mono\n\n    abs_data = np.abs(data)\n    env = np.convolve(abs_data, np.ones(1024)/1024, mode='same')\n    max_env = np.max(env)\n    attack_idx = np.argmax(env > 0.05 * max_env)\n    decay_idx = attack_idx + np.argmax(env[attack_idx:] > 0.8 * max_env)\n    release_idx = len(env) - np.argmax(env[::-1] > 0.05 * max_env) - 1\n    sustain_level = np.max(env[decay_idx:release_idx]) if release_idx > decay_idx else max_env\n\n    N = len(data)\n    fft = np.fft.rfft(data)\n    freq = np.fft.rfftfreq(N, 1/samplerate)\n    mag = np.abs(fft)\n    peaks, _ = find_peaks(mag, height=np.max(mag)*0.1)\n    if len(peaks) == 0:\n        fundamental = 0\n    else:\n        fundamental = freq[peaks[0]]\n\n    harmonics = []\n    for i in range(1, num_harmonics+1):\n        target_freq = fundamental * i\n        idx = np.argmin(np.abs(freq - target_freq))\n        harmonics.append((freq[idx], mag[idx]/np.max(mag) if np.max(mag) else 0))\n\n    with open(synth_data_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# Synthesizer Data generated from {os.path.basename(wav_path)}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Fundamental_Frequency: {fundamental:.2f} Hz\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Envelope:\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Attack: {attack_idx/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Decay: {(decay_idx-attack_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Sustain_Level: {sustain_level:.3f}\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"  Release: {(len(env)-release_idx)/samplerate:.3f} s\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Harmonics:\\n\")\n        for i, (freq_h, mag_h) in enumerate(harmonics, 1):\n            f.write(f\"  Harmonic_{i}: {freq_h:.2f} Hz, {mag_h:.3f} (relative)\\n\")\n\ndef fine_tune_instrument(config_path, tuning_cents=0):\n    if not os.path.exists(config_path):\n        return\n    with open(config_path, 'r') as f:\n        lines = f.readlines()\n\n    new_lines = []\n    found = False\n    for line in lines:\n        if line.strip().startswith('tuning_cents'):\n            new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n            found = True\n        else:\n            new_lines.append(line)\n    if not found:\n        new_lines.append(f\"tuning_cents={tuning_cents}\\n\")\n\n    with open(config_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.writelines(new_lines)\n\ndef generate_explanatory_doc(output_path, midi_scripts, wav_files, synth_data_files, instrument_configs):\n    from datetime import datetime\n    with open(output_path, 'w') as f:\n        f.write(f\"# MIDI & Synthesizer Configuration Summary\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"Generated on {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\\n\\n\")\n        f.write(f\"## Optimized MIDI Scripts\\n\")\n        for script in midi_scripts:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(script)}: Optimized for redundant CC removal and event merging.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Synthesizer Data Files\\n\")\n        for wav, synth in zip(wav_files, synth_data_files):\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(synth)}: Generated from {os.path.basename(wav)} with analyzed pitch, envelope, and harmonics.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n## Virtual Instrument Configurations\\n\")\n        for config in instrument_configs:\n            f.write(f\"- {os.path.basename(config)}: Fine-tuned for cent-level pitch adjustment.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"\\n---\\n\")\n        f.write(\"### Notes\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- MIDI scripts are optimized for efficiency and minimal latency.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Synthesizer data files can be imported into most additive/subtractive synths.\\n\")\n        f.write(\"- Instrument configuration files should be loaded into your DAW's virtual instrument plugin.\\n\")\n\nclass TestMidiAudioToolkit(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.test_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()\n\n    def tearDown(self):\n        shutil.rmtree(self.test_dir)\n\n    # -----------------     \"# Test MIDI script\",\n            \"control_change channel=0 control=7 value=100\",\n            \"control_change channel=0 control=7 value=100\",  # redundant\n            \"control_change     with open(opt_path) as f:\n            result = [l.strip() for l in f.readlines() if l.strip() and not l.startswith(\"#\")]\n\n        # Redundant CCs should be removed\n        expected_msgs = ----------------- analyze_wav_to_synth_data tests -----------------\n    def test_analyze_wav_to_synth_data_sine_wave(self):\n        # Generate a 440 Hz sine wave\n        samplerate = 44100\n        duration = 1.0\n        t = np.linspace(0, duration, int(samplerate*duration), endpoint=False)\n        freq = 440.0\n        sine = 0.5 * np.sin(2 * np.pi * freq * t)\n        wav_path = os.path.join(self.test_dir, \"sine.wav\")\n        synth_path = os.path.join(self.test_dir, \"sine.synth.txt\")\n        sf.write(wav_path, sine, samplerate)\n self.assertIn(\"Fundamental_Frequency:\", synth_lines)\n        import re\n        m = re.search(r\"Fundamental_Frequency:\\s*([0-9.]+)\", synth_lines)\n        self.assertIsNotNone(m)\n        freq_found = float(m.group(1))\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(freq_found, 440, delta=5)\n\n    def test_analyze_wav_to_synth_data_handles_stereo(self):\n        # Stereo file, both channels are the
